SELECT DISTINCT customer.c_custkey AS customer_c_custkey, lineitem.l_shipdate AS lineitem_l_shipdate, orders.o_orderdate AS orders_o_orderdate, lineitem.l_discount AS lineitem_l_discount, lineitem.l_extendedprice AS lineitem_l_extendedprice, lineitem.l_linenumber AS lineitem_l_linenumber, orders.o_orderkey AS orders_o_orderkey, orders.o_shippriority AS orders_o_shippriority FROM lineitem JOIN orders JOIN customer WHERE lineitem.l_orderkey=orders.o_orderkey AND orders.o_custkey=customer.c_custkey
SELECT DISTINCT partsupp.ps_partkey AS partsupp_ps_partkey, lineitem.l_linenumber AS lineitem_l_linenumber, lineitem.l_quantity AS lineitem_l_quantity, lineitem.l_extendedprice AS lineitem_l_extendedprice FROM partsupp JOIN lineitem WHERE lineitem.l_partkey=partsupp.ps_partkey AND lineitem.l_suppkey=partsupp.ps_suppkey 
SELECT DISTINCT lineitem.l_linenumber AS lineitem_l_linenumber, part.p_partkey AS part_p_partkey, partsupp.ps_partkey AS partsupp_ps_partkey, part.p_type AS part_p_type FROM lineitem JOIN part JOIN partsupp WHERE lineitem.l_partkey=partsupp.ps_partkey AND lineitem.l_suppkey=partsupp.ps_suppkey  AND partsupp.ps_partkey=part.p_partkey
SELECT DISTINCT region.r_name AS region_r_name, region.r_regionkey AS region_r_regionkey, orders.o_orderdate AS orders_o_orderdate, lineitem.l_extendedprice AS lineitem_l_extendedprice, lineitem.l_discount AS lineitem_l_discount, customer.c_custkey AS customer_c_custkey, lineitem.l_linenumber AS lineitem_l_linenumber, nation.n_nationkey AS nation_n_nationkey, orders.o_orderkey AS orders_o_orderkey, nation.n_name AS nation_n_name FROM lineitem JOIN orders JOIN customer JOIN nation JOIN region WHERE lineitem.l_orderkey=orders.o_orderkey AND orders.o_custkey=customer.c_custkey AND customer.c_nationkey=nation.n_nationkey AND nation.n_regionkey=region.r_regionkey
